Max boost will vary based on several factors, including, but not limited to: thermal paste; system cooling; motherboard design and BIOS; the latest AMD chipset driver; and the latest OS updates. GD-150.</p>

AMD Ryzen 3400G and 3200G series processors are not compatible. Because Precision Boost Overdrive enables operation of the processor outside of AMDâs published specifications, use of the feature invalidates the AMD product warranty and may also void warranties offered by the system manufacturer or retailer. Availability of Precision Boost Overdrive in pre-built OEM desktop systems will vary based on the PC manufacturerâs settings. Check with the PC manufacturer prior to purchase. GD-179.  </p>

GD-122\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\t\t\t\t\t\u003Cp class=\"note_detail\"\u003E2. Max boost for AMD Ryzen processors is the maximum frequency achievable by a single core on the processor running a bursty single-threaded workload. Max boost will vary based on several factors, including, but not limited to: thermal paste; system cooling; motherboard design and BIOS; the latest AMD chipset driver; and the latest OS updates. GD-150.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\t\t\t\t\t\u003Cp class=\"note_detail\"\u003E3. Precision Boost Overdrive requires an AMD Ryzen Threadripper or a Ryzen 3000\u002F4000\u002F5000 series desktop processor, and a compatible motherboard. AMD Ryzen 3400G and 3200G series processors are not compatible. Because Precision Boost Overdrive enables operation of the processor outside of AMDâs published specifications, use of the feature invalidates the AMD product warranty and may also void warranties offered by the system manufacturer or retailer. Availability of Precision Boost Overdrive in pre-built OEM desktop systems will vary based on the PC manufacturerâs settings. Check with the PC manufacturer prior to purchase.
